style="background-color:#f9f9f9;border:1px solid #aaa;color:#000">\n<tbody><tr>\n<td class="mbox-image"><img alt="" data-file-width="1024" data-file-height="1376" /></td>\n<td class="mbox-text plainlist">Wikimedia Commons has media related to <i><b><a href="https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Category:1924" href="/wiki/Leap_year" title="Leap year">leap year</a> <a href="/wiki/Leap_year_starting_on_Tuesday" title="Leap year starting on Tuesday">starting on Tuesday</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Gregorian_calendar" title="Gregorian calendar">Gregorian calendar</a>, the 1924th year of the <a href="/wiki/Common_Era" title="Common Era">Common Era</a> (CE) and <i><a href="/wiki/Anno_Domini" title="Anno Domini">Anno Domini</a></i> (AD) designations, the 924th  year of the <a href="/wiki/2nd_millennium" title="2nd millennium">2nd&#160;millennium</a>, the 24th  year of the <a href="/wiki/20th_century" title="20th century">20th&#160;century</a>, and the  5th   year of the <a href="/wiki/1920s" title="1920s">1920s</a> decade.\n</p>\n<div class="toclimit-2"><div id="Events">Events</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1924&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January">January</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1924&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: January">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:242px;"><a href="/wiki/File:1924WOlympicPoster.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5c/1924WOlympicPoster.jpg/240px-1924WOlympicPoster.jpg" width="240" height="332" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/5/5c/1924WOlympicPoster.jpg 1.5x" data-file-width="276" data-file-height="382" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:1924WOlympicPoster.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/1924_Winter_Olympics" title="1924 Winter Olympics">1924 Winter Olympics</a></div></div></div>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/January_1924" title="January 1924">January 1924</a></div>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/January_10" title="January 10">January 10</a> &#8211; The British submarine <i><a href="/wiki/HMS_L24" title="HMS L24">L-24</a></i> sinks in the <a href="/wiki/English_Channel" title="English Channel">English Channel</a>; 43 lives are lost.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/January_12" title="January 12">January 12</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Gopinath_Saha" title="Gopinath Saha">Gopinath Saha</a> shoots a man he erroneously thinks is <a href="/wiki/Charles_Tegart" title="Charles Tegart">Sir Charles Tegart</a>, the police commissioner of <a href="/wiki/Calcutta" class="mw-redirect" title="Calcutta">Calcutta</a>, and is arrested soon after.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/January_21" title="January 21">January 21</a>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Alexander_Cambridge,_1st_Earl_of_Athlone" title="Alexander Cambridge, 1st Earl of Athlone">The Earl of Athlone</a> is appointed <a href="/wiki/Governor-General_of_the_Union_of_South_Africa" class="mw-redirect" title="Governor-General of the Union of South Africa">Governor-General of the Union of South Africa</a>, and <a href="/wiki/High_Commissioner_for_Southern_Africa" title="High Commissioner for Southern Africa">High Commissioner for Southern Africa</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Union_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Union-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>Following the death of <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Lenin" title="Vladimir Lenin">Vladimir Lenin</a>, <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Stalin" title="Joseph Stalin">Joseph Stalin</a> immediately begins to purge his rivals to clear the way for his leadership.</li></ul></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/January_22" title="January 22">January 22</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Ramsay_MacDonald" title="Ramsay MacDonald">Ramsay MacDonald</a> becomes the first <a href="/wiki/Labour_Party_(UK)" title="Labour Party (UK)">Labour</a> <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_the_United_Kingdom" title="Prime Minister of the United Kingdom">Prime Minister of the United Kingdom</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/January_23" title="January 23">January 23</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet Union</a> officially declares that <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Lenin" title="Vladimir Lenin">Lenin</a> died <a href="/wiki/January_21" title="January 21">January 21</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/January_25" title="January 25">January 25</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/1924_Winter_Olympics" title="1924 Winter Olympics">1924 Winter Olympics</a> open in <a href="/wiki/Chamonix" title="Chamonix">Chamonix</a>, in the French <a href="/wiki/Alps" title="Alps">Alps</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/January_26" title="January 26">January 26</a> &#8211; Petrograd (<a href="/wiki/Saint_Petersburg" title="Saint Petersburg">Saint Petersburg</a>) is renamed <a href="/wiki/Leningrad" class="mw-redirect" title="Leningrad">Leningrad</a>; it reverts to Saint Petersburg in <a href="/wiki/1991" title="1991">1991</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/January_27" title="January 27">January 27</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Vladimir_Lenin" title="Vladimir Lenin">Lenin</a> is buried in <a href="/wiki/Lenin%27s_Mausoleum" title="Lenin&#39;s Mausoleum">Lenin\'s Mausoleum</a>, in Moscow\'s <a href="/wiki/Red_Square" title="Red Square">Red Square</a>.</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="February">February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1924&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/February_1924" title="February 1924">February 1924</a></div>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/February_1" title="February 1">February 1</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">United Kingdom</a> recognizes the <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet Union</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/February_5" title="February 5">February 5</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/GMT" class="mw-redirect" title="GMT">GMT</a>: A radio time signal is broadcast for the first time, from the <a href="/wiki/Royal_Greenwich_Observatory" class="mw-redirect" title="Royal Greenwich Observatory">Royal Greenwich Observatory</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/February_8" title="February 8">February 8</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Capital_punishment" title="Capital punishment">Capital punishment</a>: The first state execution using <a href="/wiki/Gas" title="Gas">gas</a>, in the United States, takes place in <a href="/wiki/Nevada" title="Nevada">Nevada</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/February_12" title="February 12">February 12</a> &#8211; <i><a href="/wiki/Rhapsody_in_Blue" title="Rhapsody in Blue">Rhapsody in Blue</a></i>, by <a href="/wiki/George_Gershwin" title="George Gershwin">George Gershwin</a>, is first performed in New York City, at <a href="/wiki/Aeolian_Hall_(Manhattan)" title="Aeolian Hall (Manhattan)">Aeolian Hall</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/February_14" title="February 14">February 14</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/Computing-Tabulating-Recording_Company" title="Computing-Tabulating-Recording Company">Computing-Tabulating-Recording Company</a> (CTR), based in the U.S. state of New York, is renamed <a href="/wiki/IBM" title="IBM">International Business Machines (IBM)</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/February_16" title="February 16">February 16</a>-<a href="/wiki/February_26" title="February 26">26</a> &#8211; Dock strikes break out in various U.S. harbors.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/February_22" title="February 22">February 22</a>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Treaty_of_Rome_(1924)" title="Treaty of Rome (1924)">Treaty of Rome</a>: The <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Italy" title="Kingdom of Italy">Kingdom of Italy</a> annexes the <a href="/wiki/Free_State_of_Fiume" title="Free State of Fiume">Free State of Fiume</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Serbs,_Croats_and_Slovenes" class="mw-redirect" title="Kingdom of Serbs, Croats and Slovenes">Kingdom of Serbs, Croats and Slovenes</a> absorbs <a href="/wiki/Su%C5%A1ak,_Rijeka" title="Su\xc5\xa1ak, Rijeka">Su\xc5\xa1ak</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a> becomes the first <a href="/wiki/President_of_the_United_States" title="President of the United States">President of the United States</a> to deliver a radio broadcast from the <a href="/wiki/White_House" title="White House">White House</a>.</li></ul></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="March">March</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1924&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: March">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/March_1924" title="March 1924">March 1924</a></div>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/March_3" title="March 3">March 3</a>\n<ul><li>The 407-year-old Islamic caliphate is abolished, when <a href="/wiki/List_of_caliphs#Ottoman_Caliphate_(1517_\xe2\x80\x93_3_March_1924)" class="mw-redirect" title="List of caliphs">Caliph</a> <a href="/wiki/Abd%C3%BClmecid_II" class="mw-redirect" title="Abd\xc3\xbclmecid II">Abd\xc3\xbclmecid II</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Ottoman_Caliphate" title="Ottoman Caliphate">Ottoman Caliphate</a> is deposed. The last remnant of the old regime gives way to the reformed <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a> of President <a href="/wiki/Kemal_Atat%C3%BCrk" class="mw-redirect" title="Kemal Atat\xc3\xbcrk">Kemal Atat\xc3\xbcrk</a>.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/wiki/Free_State_of_Fiume" title="Free State of Fiume">Free State of Fiume</a> is annexed by the <a href="/wiki/Kingdom_of_Italy" title="Kingdom of Italy">Kingdom of Italy</a>.</li></ul></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/March_6" title="March 6">March 6</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/%C4%B0smet_%C4%B0n%C3%B6n%C3%BC" title="\xc4\xb0smet \xc4\xb0n\xc3\xb6n\xc3\xbc">\xc4\xb0smet \xc4\xb0n\xc3\xb6n\xc3\xbc</a> forms a new government in Turkey (2nd government).</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/March_8" title="March 8">March 8</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/Castle_Gate_Mine_disaster" title="Castle Gate Mine disaster">Castle Gate Mine disaster</a> kills 172 coal miners in <a href="/wiki/Utah" title="Utah">Utah</a>, United States.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/March_25" title="March 25">March 25</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/Second_Hellenic_Republic" title="Second Hellenic Republic">Second Hellenic Republic</a> is proclaimed in Greece.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/March_29" title="March 29">March 29</a> &#8211; In France, the Third Ministry of <a href="/wiki/Raymond_Poincar%C3%A9" title="Raymond Poincar\xc3\xa9">Raymond Poincar\xc3\xa9</a> begins.</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="April">April</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1924&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: April">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/April_1924" title="April 1924">April 1924</a></div>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/April_1" title="April 1">April 1</a>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Adolf_Hitler" title="Adolf Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a> is sentenced to 5 years in jail, for his participation in the <a href="/wiki/Beer_Hall_Putsch" title="Beer Hall Putsch">Beer Hall Putsch</a> (he serves only 8 months).</li>\n<li>The first revenue flight for Belgium\'s <a href="/wiki/Sabena" title="Sabena">Sabena</a> Airlines takes place.</li></ul></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/April_6" title="April 6">April 6</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Fascist" class="mw-redirect" title="Fascist">Fascists</a> <a href="/wiki/Italian_general_election,_1924" title="Italian general election, 1924">win the elections</a> in Italy with a \xe2\x85\x94 majority.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/April_13" title="April 13">April 13</a>\n<ul><li>A <a href="/wiki/Greek_republic_referendum,_1924" title="Greek republic referendum, 1924">referendum</a> in Greece favors the formation of the <a href="/wiki/Second_Hellenic_Republic" title="Second Hellenic Republic">Second Hellenic Republic</a>.</li>\n<li>The <i><a href="/wiki/A.E.K._(sports_club)" title="A.E.K. (sports club)">A.E.K.</a></i> is founded in Greece.</li></ul></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/April_16" title="April 16">April 16</a> &#8211; American <a href="/wiki/Mass_media" title="Mass media">media</a> company <i><a href="/wiki/Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer" title="Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer">Metro-Goldwyn-Mayer</a></i> (<i>MGM</i>) is founded in <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">Los Angeles</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/April_23" title="April 23">April 23</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/British_Empire_Exhibition" title="British Empire Exhibition">British Empire Exhibition</a> opens; it is the largest <a href="/wiki/Colonial_exhibition" title="Colonial exhibition">colonial exhibition</a>, with 58 countries of the empire dramatically represented.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/April_26" title="April 26">April 26</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Harry_Grindell_Matthews" title="Harry Grindell Matthews">Harry Grindell Matthews</a> demonstrates his "<a href="/wiki/Death_ray" title="Death ray">death ray</a>" in London, but fails to convince the British <a href="/wiki/War_Office" title="War Office">War Office</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/April_27" title="April 27">April 27</a> &#8211; A group of <a href="/wiki/Alawites" title="Alawites">Alawites</a> kill several <a href="/wiki/Nun" title="Nun">nuns</a> in <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>; French troops march against them.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/April_28" title="April 28">April 28</a> &#8211; An explosion in a mine at the Wheeling Steel Corporation in <a href="/wiki/Benwood,_West_Virginia" title="Benwood, West Virginia">Benwood, West Virginia</a> kills 119 men.</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="May">May</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1924&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: May">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/May_1924" title="May 1924">May 1924</a></div>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/May_3" title="May 3">May 3</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/Aleph_Zadik_Aleph" title="Aleph Zadik Aleph">Aleph Zadik Aleph</a>, the oldest Jewish youth fraternity, is founded in <a href="/wiki/Omaha,_Nebraska" title="Omaha, Nebraska">Omaha, Nebraska</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/May_4" title="May 4">May 4</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/1924_Summer_Olympics" title="1924 Summer Olympics">1924 Summer Olympics</a> opening ceremonies are held in Paris, France.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/May_8" title="May 8">May 8</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Lithuania" title="Lithuania">Lithuania</a> signs the <a href="/wiki/Klaip%C4%97da_Convention" title="Klaip\xc4\x97da Convention">Klaip\xc4\x97da Convention</a> with the nations of the <a href="/wiki/Conference_of_Ambassadors" title="Conference of Ambassadors">Conference of Ambassadors</a>, taking the <a href="/wiki/Klaip%C4%97da_Region" title="Klaip\xc4\x97da Region">Klaip\xc4\x97da Region</a> from <a href="/wiki/East_Prussia" title="East Prussia">East Prussia</a>, and making it into an autonomous region.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/May_10" title="May 10">May 10</a> &#8211; In the United States, <a href="/wiki/J._Edgar_Hoover" title="J. Edgar Hoover">J. Edgar Hoover</a> is appointed head of the Federal <a href="/wiki/Bureau_of_Investigation" class="mw-redirect" title="Bureau of Investigation">Bureau of Investigation</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/May_11" title="May 11">May 11</a> &#8211; <i><a href="/wiki/Mercedes-Benz" title="Mercedes-Benz">Mercedes-Benz</a></i> is formed by the merging companies owned by <a href="/wiki/Gottlieb_Daimler" title="Gottlieb Daimler">Gottlieb Daimler</a> and <a href="/wiki/Karl_Benz" title="Karl Benz">Karl Benz</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/May_21" title="May 21">May 21</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/University_of_Chicago" title="University of Chicago">University of Chicago</a> students <a href="/wiki/Leopold_and_Loeb" title="Leopold and Loeb">Richard Loeb and Nathan Leopold, Jr.</a> murder 14-year-old <a href="/wiki/Bobby_Franks" class="mw-redirect" title="Bobby Franks">Bobby Franks</a>, in a <a href="/wiki/Thrill_killing" title="Thrill killing">thrill killing</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/May_24" title="May 24">May 24</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/Immigration_Act_of_1924" title="Immigration Act of 1924">Immigration Act of 1924</a> is signed into law in the United States, including the <a href="/wiki/Asian_Exclusion_Act" class="mw-redirect" title="Asian Exclusion Act">Asian Exclusion Act</a>.</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="June">June</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1924&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: June">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/June_1924" title="June 1924">June 1924</a></div>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/June_1" title="June 1">June 1</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Harry_Grindell_Matthews" title="Harry Grindell Matthews">Harry Grindell Matthews</a> returns from Paris to London; he tries to use a <i><a href="/wiki/Path%C3%A9" title="Path\xc3\xa9">Path\xc3\xa9</a></i> film to demonstrate that his <a href="/wiki/Death_ray" title="Death ray">death ray</a> works.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/June_2" title="June 2">June 2</a> &#8211; U.S. President <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a> signs the <a href="/wiki/Indian_Citizenship_Act" title="Indian Citizenship Act">Indian Citizenship Act</a> into law, granting <a href="/wiki/Citizenship" title="Citizenship">citizenship</a> to all <a href="/wiki/Native_Americans_in_the_United_States" title="Native Americans in the United States">Native Americans</a> born within the territorial limits of the United States.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/June_5" title="June 5">June 5</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Ernst_Alexanderson" title="Ernst Alexanderson">Ernst Alexanderson</a> sends the first <a href="/wiki/Fax" title="Fax">facsimile</a> across the <a href="/wiki/Atlantic_Ocean" title="Atlantic Ocean">Atlantic Ocean</a>, which goes to his father in <a href="/wiki/Sweden" title="Sweden">Sweden</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/June_8" title="June 8">June 8</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/George_Mallory" title="George Mallory">George Mallory</a> and <a href="/wiki/Andrew_Irvine_(mountaineer)" title="Andrew Irvine (mountaineer)">Andrew Irvine</a> are last seen "going strong for the top" of <a href="/wiki/Mount_Everest" title="Mount Everest">Mount Everest</a> by teammate <a href="/wiki/Noel_Odell" title="Noel Odell">Noel Odell</a> at 12:50&#160;P.M. The two <a href="/wiki/Mountaineering" title="Mountaineering">mountaineers</a> are never seen alive again.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/June_10" title="June 10">June 10</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Fascist" class="mw-redirect" title="Fascist">Fascists</a> kidnap and kill Italian socialist leader <a href="/wiki/Giacomo_Matteotti" title="Giacomo Matteotti">Giacomo Matteotti</a> in Rome.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/June_12" title="June 12">June 12</a> &#8211; Rondout Heist: Six men of the <a href="/wiki/Egan%27s_Rats" title="Egan&#39;s Rats">Egan\'s Rats</a> gang rob a mail train in <a href="/wiki/Rondout,_Illinois" title="Rondout, Illinois">Rondout, Illinois</a>; the robbery is later found to have been an inside job.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/June_13" title="June 13">June 13</a> &#8211; In Hungary, a most devastating tornado called "Wildkansas" strikes, leaving a 500-1500m wide and 70&#160;km long path of destruction, lands at Bia, and after 3 hours it ends near V\xc3\xa1c, destroys a village called P\xc3\xa1ty completely, and leaves many people homeless, kills 9 people, and 50 people got wounded. This was one of the strongest tornadoes ever not only in Hungary but in Europe also. It was estimated to be an F4.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/June_16" title="June 16">June 16</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Whampoa_Military_Academy" class="mw-redirect" title="Whampoa Military Academy">Whampoa Military Academy</a> is founded in China.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/June_23" title="June 23">June 23</a> &#8211; American airman <a href="/wiki/Russell_Maughan" title="Russell Maughan">Russell Maughan</a> flies from New York to San Francisco in 21 hours and 48&#160;minutes on a dawn-to-dusk flight in a Curtiss pursuit.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/June_28" title="June 28">June 28</a> &#8211; A tornado touches down in <a href="/wiki/Lorain,_Ohio" title="Lorain, Ohio">Lorain, Ohio</a> and kills 78 people.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/June_30" title="June 30">June 30</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/James_Barry_Munnik_Hertzog" class="mw-redirect" title="James Barry Munnik Hertzog">J.B.M. Hertzog</a> becomes the third <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_South_Africa" title="Prime Minister of South Africa">Prime Minister of South Africa</a>.</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="July">July</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1924&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: July">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/July_1924" title="July 1924">July 1924</a></div>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/July_9" title="July 9">July 9</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/John_W._Davis" title="John W. The constitutional government headed by General <a href="/wiki/Horacio_V%C3%A1squez" title="Horacio V\xc3\xa1squez">Horacio V\xc3\xa1zquez</a>, elected in the elections held in March, is established.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/July_19" title="July 19">July 19</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/Napalp%C3%AD_massacre" title="Napalp\xc3\xad massacre">Napalp\xc3\xad massacre</a> occurs in <a href="/wiki/Argentina" title="Argentina">Argentina</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/July_20" title="July 20">July 20</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet</a> sports newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/Sovetsky_Sport" title="Sovetsky Sport">Sovetsky Sport</a></i> is founded.</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="August">August</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1924&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: August">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/August_1924" title="August 1924">August 1924</a></div>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/August_1" title="August 1">August 1</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Koshien_Stadium" title="Koshien Stadium">Koshien Stadium</a>, as well known for sports venues in <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>, open in <a href="/wiki/Nishinomiya" title="Nishinomiya">Nishinomiya</a>, suburb of <a href="/wiki/Osaka" title="Osaka">Osaka</a>. <sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup><sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. The <a href="/wiki/Geneva_Protocol_(1924)" title="Geneva Protocol (1924)">Geneva Protocol</a> is adopted by the <a href="/wiki/League_of_Nations" title="League of Nations">League of Nations</a> Assembly as a means to strengthen the League, but later fails to be ratified.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/October_10" title="October 10">October 10</a>\n<ul><li>Voting in federal elections becomes compulsory in Australia, after a private member\'s bill proposed by <a href="/wiki/Tasmania" title="Tasmania">Tasmanian</a> <a href="/wiki/National_Party_of_Australia" title="National Party of Australia">Nationalist</a> senator Herbert Payne results in the passing of the Commonwealth Electoral (Compulsory Voting) Act 1924.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/wiki/Alpha_Delta_Gamma" title="Alpha Delta Gamma">Alpha Delta Gamma</a> fraternity is founded at the Lake Shore Campus of <a href="/wiki/Loyola_University_Chicago" title="Loyola University Chicago">Loyola University</a>, Chicago.</li></ul></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/October_12" title="October 12">October 12</a>&#8211; The first <a href="/wiki/Surrealist_Manifesto" title="Surrealist Manifesto">Surrealist Manifesto</a> is published, in which <a href="/wiki/Andr%C3%A9_Breton" title="Andr\xc3\xa9 Breton">Andr\xc3\xa9 Breton</a> defines the movement as "pure psychic <a href="/wiki/Surrealist_automatism" title="Surrealist automatism">automatism</a>".</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/October_18" title="October 18">October 18</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Prime_Minister_of_Sweden" title="Prime Minister of Sweden">Sweden\'s Prime Minister</a> <a href="/wiki/Ernst_Trygger" title="Ernst Trygger">Ernst Trygger</a> and his cabinet, is replaced by Hjalmar Branting and his third and last government.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/October_19" title="October 19">October 19</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Ibn_Saud" title="Ibn Saud">Abdul Aziz</a> declares himself protector of holy places in <a href="/wiki/Mecca" title="Mecca">Mecca</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/October_22" title="October 22">October 22</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/Toastmasters_International" title="Toastmasters International">Toastmasters</a> Club is founded.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/October_24" title="October 24">October 24</a>\n<ul><li>The British Foreign Office publishes the <a href="/wiki/Zinoviev_letter" title="Zinoviev letter">Zinoviev letter</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Dixie_Dean" title="Dixie Dean">Dixie Dean</a> scores a <a href="/wiki/Hat-trick#Association_football" title="Hat-trick">hat-trick</a> for <a href="/wiki/Tranmere_Rovers_F.C." title="Tranmere Rovers F.C.">Tranmere Rovers</a> to become the youngest ever player to score three goals for The Superwhites.</li></ul></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/October_25" title="October 25">October 25</a> &#8211; British authorities in India arrest <a href="/wiki/Subhas_Chandra_Bose" title="Subhas Chandra Bose">Subhas Chandra Bose</a> and jail him for the next 2\xc2\xbd years.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/October_27" title="October 27">October 27</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/Uzbek_SSR" class="mw-redirect" title="Uzbek SSR">Uzbek SSR</a> joins the Soviet Union.</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="November">November</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1924&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: November">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/November_1924" title="November 1924">November 1924</a></div>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/November_4" title="November 4">November 4</a>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Nellie_Tayloe_Ross" title="Nellie Tayloe Ross">Nellie Tayloe Ross</a> of <a href="/wiki/Wyoming" title="Wyoming">Wyoming</a> is elected as the first woman governor in the United States.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/U.S._presidential_election,_1924" class="mw-redirect" title="U.S. presidential election, 1924">U.S. presidential election, 1924</a>: Republican <a href="/wiki/Calvin_Coolidge" title="Calvin Coolidge">Calvin Coolidge</a> defeats Democrat <a href="/wiki/John_W._Davis" title="John W. La Follette, Sr.</a></li></ul></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/November_19" title="November 19">November 19</a> &#8211; In <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">Los Angeles</a>, famous <a href="/wiki/Silent_film" title="Silent film">silent film</a> director <a href="/wiki/Thomas_H._Ince" title="Thomas H. Ince">Thomas Ince</a> ("The Father of the Western") dies, reportedly of a <a href="/wiki/Myocardial_infarction" title="Myocardial infarction">heart attack</a>, in his bed (rumors soon surface that he was shot dead by publishing tycoon <a href="/wiki/William_Randolph_Hearst" title="William Randolph Hearst">William Randolph Hearst</a>).</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/November_21" title="November 21">November 21</a> &#8211; <a href="/wiki/Ali_Fethi_Okyar" class="mw-redirect" title="Ali Fethi Okyar">Ali Fethi Okyar</a> forms new government in <a href="/wiki/Turkey" title="Turkey">Turkey</a>. (3rd government)</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/November_26" title="November 26">November 26</a> &#8211; The <a href="/wiki/Mongolian_People%27s_Republic" title="Mongolian People&#39;s Republic">Mongolian People\'s Republic</a> is founded.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/November_27" title="November 27">November 27</a>\n<ul><li>129 communists, including several members of the <a href="/wiki/Riigikogu" held.</li></ul></li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="December">December</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1924&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: December">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/December_1924" title="December 1924">December 1924</a></div>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/December_1" title="December 1">December 1</a>\n<ul><li>A Soviet-backed communist <a href="/wiki/1924_Estonian_coup_d%27%C3%A9tat_attempt" title="1924 Estonian coup d&#39;\xc3\xa9tat attempt">coup attempt</a> fails in <a href="/wiki/Estonia" title="Estonia">Estonia</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/George_Gershwin" title="George Gershwin">George Gershwin</a>\'s <i><a href="/wiki/Oh,_Lady_Be_Good!" title="Oh, Lady Be Good!">Lady Be Good</a></i> and <i><a href="/wiki/Fascinating_Rhythm" title="Fascinating Rhythm">Fascinating Rhythm</a></i> (book by <a href="/wiki/Guy_Bolton" title="Guy Bolton">Guy Bolton</a> and <a href="/wiki/Fred_Thompson" title="Fred Thompson">Fred Thompson</a>, lyrics by <a href="/wiki/Ira_Gershwin" title="Ira Gershwin">Ira Gershwin</a>) premiere in New York, NY.</li></ul></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/December_19" title="December 19">December 19</a>\n<ul><li>German serial killer <a href="/wiki/Fritz_Haarmann" title="Fritz Haarmann">Fritz Haarmann</a> is sentenced to death for a series of murders.</li>\n<li>The last <a href="/wiki/Rolls-Royce_Silver_Ghost" title="Rolls-Royce Silver Ghost">Rolls-Royce Silver Ghost</a> is sold in London, England.</li></ul></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/December_20" title="December 20">December 20</a> &#8211; In Germany, <a href="/wiki/Adolf_Hitler" title="Adolf Hitler">Adolf Hitler</a> is released from Landsberg Prison, after serving nine months for his crucial role in the <a href="/wiki/Beer_Hall_Putsch" title="Beer Hall Putsch">Beer Hall Putsch</a>, from <a href="/wiki/1923" title="1923">1923</a>.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/December_24" title="December 24">December 24</a>\n<ul><li>An <a href="/wiki/1924_Imperial_Airways_de_Havilland_DH.34_crash" title="1924 Imperial Airways de Havilland DH.34 crash">air crash</a> at <a href="/wiki/Croydon_Airport" title="Croydon Airport">Croydon Air Field</a> in London kills 8.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Albania" title="Albania">Albania</a> becomes a <a href="/wiki/Republic" title="Republic">republic</a>.</li>\n<li>A <a href="/wiki/Babbs_Switch_fire" title="Babbs Switch fire">flash fire</a> at a Christmas celebration in a one-room schoolhouse in <a href="/wiki/Babbs,_Oklahoma" title="Babbs, Oklahoma">Babbs, Oklahoma</a> kills 36 people, mostly small children.</li></ul></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/December_30" title="December 30">December 30</a> &#8211; Astronomer <a href="/wiki/Edwin_Hubble" title="Edwin Hubble">Edwin Hubble</a> announces that <a href="/wiki/Andromeda_Galaxy" title="Andromeda Galaxy">Andromeda</a>, previously believed to be a <a href="/wiki/Nebula" title="Nebula">nebula</a>, is actually another <a href="/wiki/Galaxy" title="Galaxy">galaxy</a>, and that the <a href="/wiki/Milky_Way" title="Milky Way">Milky Way</a> is only one of many such galaxies in the <a href="/wiki/Universe" title="Universe">universe</a>.</li></ul>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Date_unknown">Date unknown</span><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>\n<ul><li>The <a href="/wiki/Taung_Child" title="Taung Child">Taung Child</a> is discovered.</li>\n<li>Spring &#8211; Francophone explorer, spiritualist and former operatic soprano <a href="/wiki/Alexandra_David-N%C3%A9el" title="Alexandra David-N\xc3\xa9el">Alexandra David-N\xc3\xa9el</a>, disguised as a male pilgrim, makes a 2-month stay in the forbidden city of <a href="/wiki/Lhasa_(prefecture-level_city)" title="Lhasa (prefecture-level city)">Lhasa</a>, Tibet.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup></li>\n<li>International Union of Official Organizations for Tourist <a href="/wiki/Propaganda" title="Propaganda">Propaganda</a>.</li>\n<li>The powerful opiate <a href="/wiki/Hydromorphone" title="Hydromorphone">hydromorphone</a> is developed in Germany.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Earl_W._Bascom" title="Earl W. Bascom">Earl W. Bascom</a>, rodeo cowboy and artist, designs and makes rodeo\'s first one-hand bareback rigging at <a href="/wiki/Stirling" title="Stirling">Stirling</a>, <a href="/wiki/Alberta" title="Alberta">Alberta</a> Canada.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Alice_Vanderbilt_Morris" title="Alice Vanderbilt Morris">Alice Vanderbilt Morris</a>, a wealthy heiress, founds the <a href="/wiki/Edward_VIII" title="Edward VIII">Edward, Prince of Wales</a> makes a state visit to Japan aboard <a href="/wiki/HMS_Renown" title="HMS Renown">HMS&#160;<i>Renown</i></a>.</li>\n<li>U.S. bootleggers begin to use <a href="/wiki/Thompson_submachine_gun" title="Thompson submachine gun">Thompson submachine guns</a>.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/wiki/Earth_inductor_compass" title="Earth inductor compass">Earth inductor compass</a> is invented in New York City.</li>\n<li>In the United States, both the <a href="/wiki/Renegade_period_of_the_Apache_Wars" class="mw-redirect" title="Renegade period of the Apache Wars">Renegade Period</a> and the <a href="/wiki/Apache_Wars" title="Apache Wars">Apache Wars</a> end, bringing the <a href="/wiki/American_Indian_Wars" title="American Indian Wars">American Indian Wars</a> to a close, after 302 years.</li>\n<li>The <a href="/wiki/National_Hockey_League" title="National Hockey League">National Hockey League</a> expands to the United States for the first time, adding the <a href="/wiki/Boston_Bruins" title="Boston Bruins">Boston Bruins</a>.</li></ul>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline"
